@keyframes bounce {
    0%, 100% {
        transform: translateY(0);
    }
    20% {
        transform: translateY(-20px);
    }
    40% {
        transform: translateY(10px);
    }
    60% {
        transform: translateY(-10px);
    }
    80% {
        transform: translateY(5px);
    }
}

@keyframes grow {
    0% {
        transform: scale(1);
    }
    50% {
        transform: scale(5.1); /* Slowly grows */
    }
    70% {
        transform: scale(6.1); /* Pops inward */
    }
    80% {
        transform: scale(6.8) translateX(-1px); /* Pops outward */
    }    
    90% {
        transform: scale(0); /* Pops outward */
    }
    100% {
        transform: scale(0); /* Returns to normal size */
    }
}
